It's under\\n18:   active development and is expected to be the successor to the gRPC :ref:`bridge filter\\n19:   <config_http_filters_grpc_bridge>`.\\n20: * gRPC-JSON transcoder is supported by a :ref:`filter <config_http_filters_grpc_json_transcoder>`\\n21:   that allows a RESTful JSON API client to send requests to Envoy over HTTP and get proxied to a\\n22:   gRPC service.\\n23: \\n24: .. _arch_overview_grpc_bridging:\\n25: \\n26: ...
